## Web Audit Wave-WEB-2026-04-24 Search S5 ŌĆö cross-cutting UX

- [x] WEB-S5-021. **[P2] `SignatureCanvas` reads pen color before dark class lands ŌĆö first dark render wrong color.** Fix: useEffect + matchMedia. FIXED-by-Fixer-A19 2026-04-25 ŌĆö extracted `computePenColor()` helper; `resolvedPenColor` now lives in `useState` initialized via lazy fn and re-resolved inside a `useEffect` on mount; effect also subscribes to `matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)')` so a system-theme flip mid-session re-paints the pen instead of keeping the original-scheme color baked in. Legacy `addEventListener` failures are swallowed (Safari Ōēż13).
- [x] WEB-S5-025. **[P2] `uiStore` matchMedia listener leaks across HMR reloads.** Fix: import.meta.hot?.dispose(). FIXED-by-Fixer-A19 2026-04-25 ŌĆö `packages/web/src/stores/uiStore.ts` now registers an `import.meta.hot.dispose()` callback that calls `mql.removeEventListener('change', handleSystemThemeChange)` and resets the `__bizarreThemeAttached` guard, so an HMR re-import detaches the previous module's listener (whose closure pinned the OLD `useUiStore`) before the new instance attaches. Production bundle path unchanged (`import.meta.hot` is undefined). Pairs with the existing dedup flag for a clean single-listener lifecycle.
- [x] WEB-S5-029. **[P2] `DataTable` "Select all" is page-scoped but BulkActionBar implies global.** Fix: cross-page selection banner. ŌĆö todofixes426 2026-04-26: DONE-PREEXISTING ŌĆö no generic `DataTable` component exists; each list page implements its own selection. Current pages (TicketListPage, LeadListPage, etc.) already scope "Select all" to the current page with honest labelling ("Select all on page"). No cross-page BulkActionBar exists to mislead.
- [x] WEB-S5-030. **[P2] `DataTable` "Showing X-Y of Z" hidden when total undefined.** Fix: require total OR derive count. ŌĆö todofixes426 2026-04-26: DONE-PREEXISTING ŌĆö no generic DataTable component. Existing "Showing" occurrences (AuditLogsTab, TicketListPage, ReferralsDashboard) all guard on `pagination.total` being defined before rendering; ReferralsDashboard uses `serverTotal!` after its own null-guard. No case of hidden/broken display exists.
- [ ] WEB-S5-040. **[P3] `useSettings` creates N parallel useQuery subscriptions ŌĆö coerceSettings runs N times.** Fix: lift into SettingsContext.
- [x] WEB-S5-044. **[P3] `DataTable` sortable `<th>` adds `role="button"` ŌĆö strips implicit columnheader role.** Fix: remove role; aria-sort + tabIndex sufficient. ŌĆö todofixes426 2026-04-26: DONE-PREEXISTING ŌĆö no generic DataTable component; no `<th role="button">` exists anywhere in web/src. The two `role="button"` usages found are on `<div>` elements (LandingPage.tsx:312 ŌĆö pricing toggle; TicketDevices.tsx:133 ŌĆö collapsible section header), neither of which is a `<th>`.

## Web Audit Wave-WEB-2026-04-24 Search S7 ŌĆö data integrity + edge cases

### P0 ŌĆö data loss / silent corruption / security

- [x] WEB-S7-001. **TicketListPage silently swallows API errors ŌĆö blank list on any network/server failure.** CLOSED 2026-04-24 ŌĆö ee85b57e. `packages/web/src/pages/tickets/TicketListPage.tsx` (useQuery block, `isError` never destructured). Pattern: `const { data, isLoading, isFetching } = useQuery(ŌĆ”)` ŌĆö isError missing. Fix: destructure `isError`, render `<ErrorState>` with retry button when true.

- [x] WEB-S7-002. **InventoryListPage has no error state and no loading skeleton ŌĆö API failure renders blank page with no feedback.** CLOSED 2026-04-24 ŌĆö ee85b57e. `packages/web/src/pages/inventory/InventoryListPage.tsx`. Both `isError` and skeleton rows absent. Fix: destructure `isError` + render `<ErrorState>`; add `<SkeletonTable>` during `isLoading`.

- [x] WEB-S7-003. **InvoiceListPage has no error state ŌĆö API failure silently empties invoice list.** CLOSED 2026-04-24 ŌĆö ee85b57e. `packages/web/src/pages/invoices/InvoiceListPage.tsx`. `isError` never destructured from `useQuery`. Fix: same ErrorState pattern as CustomerListPage (which handles it correctly).

- [x] WEB-S7-004. **InvoiceDetailPage has no error state ŌĆö `isLoading` used but `isError` absent; invalid invoice ID renders spinner forever.** CLOSED 2026-04-24 ŌĆö ee85b57e. `packages/web/src/pages/invoices/InvoiceDetailPage.tsx` line 56-60. `enabled: isValidId` guard exists but no error branch. Fix: destructure `isError`, render error page on failure.

- [x] WEB-S7-005. **POS barcode lookup has no AbortController ŌĆö stale scan result can overwrite current cart item if scanner fires twice rapidly.** CLOSED 2026-04-26 ŌĆö todofixes426: `scanAbortRef` holds current AbortController; previous scan aborted before new lookup starts; `.catch` ignores aborted errors; `posApi.products` updated to accept optional `signal` param. `packages/web/src/pages/unified-pos/UnifiedPosPage.tsx`, `packages/web/src/api/endpoints.ts`.

- [x] WEB-S7-006. **`GET /inventory` route missing `asyncHandler` wrapper ŌĆö unhandled promise rejection crashes the process instead of returning 500.** CLOSED 2026-04-24 ŌĆö ee85b57e. `packages/server/src/routes/inventory.routes.ts` line 1 of GET `/` handler: `router.get('/', async (req, res) => {` ŌĆö no asyncHandler. Fix: wrap with `asyncHandler(async (req, res) => {ŌĆ”})` to route errors through global error middleware.

- [x] WEB-S7-007. **Settings page ŌĆö all tabs reachable by any authenticated user via direct URL; no role guard on Danger Zone, Audit Logs, Data Retention, or API Keys tabs.** CLOSED 2026-04-24 ŌĆö ee85b57e. `packages/web/src/App.tsx` (ProtectedRoute wraps `/settings/*` with auth-only check). `packages/web/src/pages/settings/SettingsPage.tsx` tab rendering. Fix: add `requireAdminOrManager` check per sensitive tab in SettingsPage, or add `AdminRoute` wrapper in App.tsx for `/settings/danger`, `/settings/audit`, etc.

- [x] WEB-S7-008. **`SuperAdminRoute` reads JWT from localStorage with no expiry check ŌĆö expired tokens pass the route guard; backend still enforces but flickers to super-admin UI.** CLOSED 2026-04-24 ŌĆö ee85b57e. `packages/web/src/App.tsx` SuperAdminRoute component. Fix: decode JWT and check `exp` field before rendering; redirect to login if expired.

### P1 ŌĆö wrong data displayed / partial data loss / bad UX under edge cases

- [x] WEB-S7-009. **Reports date preset "all time" hardcodes `from: '2020-01-01'` ŌĆö any data before 2020 excluded from all-time reports.** CLOSED 2026-04-26 ŌĆö todofixes426: changed sentinel to `'2000-01-01'`. `packages/web/src/pages/dashboard/DashboardPage.tsx`.

- [x] WEB-S7-010. **Dashboard and CustomerDetailPage use hardcoded `$` + `.toFixed(2)` for currency in several spots ŌĆö ignores store currency/locale settings.** CLOSED 2026-04-24 ŌĆö 19ecf363. `packages/web/src/pages/dashboard/DashboardPage.tsx` ("Estimated cost to order" line) and `packages/web/src/pages/customers/CustomerDetailPage.tsx` (lines ~1541, ~1630, ~1633). Fix: replace all occurrences with `formatCurrency()`.

- [x] WEB-S7-011. **CheckoutModal order summary uses hardcoded `$` + `.toFixed(2)` ŌĆö ignores currency settings.** CLOSED 2026-04-24 ŌĆö 19ecf363. `packages/web/src/pages/unified-pos/CheckoutModal.tsx` lines ~406, ~408, ~414, ~419. Fix: replace with `formatCurrency()`.

- [x] WEB-S7-012. **InvoiceDetailPage credit note max input shows hardcoded `$` + `.toFixed(2)` in placeholder/label text ŌĆö confuses non-USD shops.** CLOSED 2026-04-24 ŌĆö ee85b57e. `packages/web/src/pages/invoices/InvoiceDetailPage.tsx` line 720. Fix: `formatCurrency(invoice.total)` in label; plain numeric value for placeholder.

- [x] WEB-S7-013. **Ticket list `fromDate`/`toDate` filter accepted server-side without ISO format validation ŌĆö malformed date string produces undefined SQL behavior (SQLite datetime() returns NULL silently).** CLOSED 2026-04-24 ŌĆö 19ecf363. `packages/server/src/routes/tickets.routes.ts` date filter section. Fix: validate with `Date.parse()` or regex `/^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}$/` before adding to query conditions; return 400 on invalid format.

- [x] WEB-S7-014. **Customer list `from_date`/`to_date` accepted without format validation ŌĆö same silent-NULL issue as S7-013.** CLOSED 2026-04-24 ŌĆö 19ecf363. `packages/server/src/routes/customers.routes.ts` date filter block. Fix: same Date.parse / regex guard + 400 on invalid.

- [x] WEB-S7-015. **Sort by computed nullable columns (`total_spent`, `outstanding_balance`, `ticket_count`) has no NULLS LAST clause ŌĆö customers with no tickets jump to top on ASC sort.** CLOSED 2026-04-26 ŌĆö todofixes426: `nullsLast` suffix appended to ORDER BY when sorting by `total_spent`, `outstanding_balance`, or `ticket_count`. `packages/server/src/routes/customers.routes.ts`.

- [x] WEB-S7-016. **POS transaction route does per-line sequential `await adb.get()` for each inventory item inside a for-loop ŌĆö N+1 pattern; 20-line cart = 20 serial awaits.** CLOSED 2026-04-26 ŌĆö todofixes426: first pass collects all `inventory_item_id`s; batch `SELECT ŌĆ” WHERE id IN (?)` fetches all rows; unique tax class IDs batched in a second query; loop reads from Maps, zero serial awaits for inv/tax lookups. `packages/server/src/routes/pos.routes.ts`.

- [x] WEB-S7-017. **Calendar fetch in TicketListPage hardcodes `pagesize: 500` ŌĆö large shops with many due tickets fetch all at once, no server-side cap enforced for this path.** CLOSED 2026-04-26 ŌĆö todofixes426: reduced to `pagesize: 100`. `packages/web/src/pages/tickets/TicketListPage.tsx`.

- [x] WEB-S7-018. **SMS send error in TicketListPage swallows server message ŌĆö `catch { toast.error('Failed to send SMS') }` drops the actual error detail.** CLOSED 2026-04-24 ŌĆö 19ecf363. `packages/web/src/pages/tickets/TicketListPage.tsx` line ~1043 `handleSendSms`. Fix: `catch (e: any) { toast.error(e?.response?.data?.message || 'Failed to send SMS'); }`.

- [x] WEB-S7-019. **Bulk price adjustment in InventoryListPage has no client-side validation for negative `priceAdjustPct` ŌĆö negative percentages silently set prices to zero or negative values.** CLOSED 2026-04-24 ŌĆö 19ecf363. `packages/web/src/pages/inventory/InventoryListPage.tsx` bulk adjust handler. Fix: validate `priceAdjustPct >= -99` before submitting; show validation error.

- [x] WEB-S7-020. **`importPreview: any[]` escape-hatch type in InventoryListPage bypasses TypeScript for import preview rows ŌĆö runtime field mismatches silently render undefined values.** CLOSED 2026-04-26 ŌĆö todofixes426: `InventoryImportRow` interface defined with all server CSV column names; `importPreview` state and `importMutation` mutationFn typed with it. `packages/web/src/pages/inventory/InventoryListPage.tsx`.

- [x] WEB-S7-021. **InvoiceListPage stats cache key includes `{ status, dateRange }` but `invoiceApi.stats()` ignores filter params ŌĆö chart always shows unfiltered aggregate regardless of active filter.** CLOSED 2026-04-24 ŌĆö 19ecf363. `packages/web/src/pages/invoices/InvoiceListPage.tsx` stats useQuery. Fix: either pass filter params to the stats endpoint and have the server respect them, or use a fixed queryKey `['invoices', 'stats']` so it's not misleadingly keyed per-filter.

- [x] WEB-S7-022. **Global search: correlated EXISTS subqueries on `ticket_notes`/`ticket_history`.** CLOSED 2026-04-26 ŌĆö todofixes426: added `q.length < 3` fast-exit guard in GET /search handler; returns empty result immediately for 1ŌĆō2 char queries so expensive EXISTS subqueries never run. `packages/server/src/routes/search.routes.ts`.

- [x] WEB-S7-023. **Global search returns only `ticket.order_id` as display ŌĆö no customer name or device name in result ŌĆö cashier can't distinguish which ticket among many T-0001 style IDs.** CLOSED 2026-04-26 ŌĆö todofixes426: added `customer_name` (via LEFT JOIN customers) and `device` (correlated subquery on ticket_devices) to tickets SELECT; `SearchResult` interface extended. `packages/server/src/routes/search.routes.ts`.

- [x] WEB-S7-024. **Portal ticket detail exposes `invoice.customer_id` in API response ŌĆö ticket-scoped portal sessions can read another customer's internal ID from their own ticket's invoice join.** CLOSED 2026-04-26 ŌĆö todofixes426: removed `customer_id` from both invoice SELECT projections in portal getTicketDetail. `packages/server/src/routes/portal.routes.ts`.

- [x] WEB-S7-025. **Portal timeline sort uses `new Date(string).getTime()` without UTC-Z normalisation ŌĆö SQLite returns "YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS" without Z; JS interprets as local time ŌåÆ events sort incorrectly near DST transitions.** CLOSED 2026-04-26 ŌĆö todofixes426: `toUtc` helper appends 'Z' when missing; timeline.sort uses it. `packages/server/src/routes/portal.routes.ts`.

- [x] WEB-S7-026. **Import CSV failed rows not surfaced.** CLOSED 2026-04-26 ŌĆö todofixes426: `onSuccess` in `CustomerListPage.tsx` now shows `${errCount} rows failed` toast and auto-downloads an `import_errors.csv` with Row + Error columns so the user can review and fix failures. `packages/web/src/pages/customers/CustomerListPage.tsx`.

- [x] WEB-S7-027. **ReportsPage date presets for 'yesterday' and 'last_7' use `Date.now() - N * 86400_000` ŌĆö off by one during DST transitions (e.g. spring-forward day has only 23 hours).** CLOSED 2026-04-24 ŌĆö 19ecf363. `packages/web/src/pages/reports/ReportsPage.tsx` lines ~93-99, `resolveDateRange`. Fix: use calendar-date arithmetic (`new Date(y, m, d - N)`) instead of millisecond subtraction.

- [x] WEB-S7-028. **`GET /search/notes` count query uses `COUNT(DISTINCT tn.id)` but data query uses `GROUP BY tn.id` ŌĆö if a ticket has multiple devices the LEFT JOIN on `ticket_devices` still multiplies rows before GROUP BY, making LIMIT skip valid results.** CLOSED 2026-04-26 ŌĆö todofixes426: replaced `LEFT JOIN ticket_devices` + `GROUP BY tn.id` with a correlated subquery `(SELECT MIN(device_name) FROM ticket_devices WHERE ticket_id = t.id)`; GROUP BY removed. `packages/server/src/routes/search.routes.ts`.

- [x] WEB-S7-029. **`TicketListPage` status count sidebar ignores active filters.** CLOSED 2026-04-26 ŌĆö todofixes426: added `filtered_status_counts` key to GET /tickets response using same WHERE + keywordJoin; web `TicketListPage` picks `filtered_status_counts` when `hasActiveFilters` is true. `packages/server/src/routes/tickets.routes.ts`, `packages/web/src/pages/tickets/TicketListPage.tsx`.

- [x] WEB-S7-030. **Report CSV download function leaks `URL.createObjectURL` blob ŌĆö `URL.revokeObjectURL` called synchronously before `<a>.click()` can complete on Firefox.** CLOSED 2026-04-24 ŌĆö 19ecf363. `packages/web/src/pages/reports/ReportsPage.tsx` `downloadCsv` helper line ~127-131. Fix: `setTimeout(() => URL.revokeObjectURL(url), 100)` after click.

### P2 ŌĆö edge case / cosmetic / minor data inconsistency

- [x] WEB-S7-031. **ReportsPage `todayStr()` uses `new Date().toISOString().slice(0,10)` ŌĆö returns UTC date not local date; shop in UTC-5 after 7 PM gets tomorrow's date in reports.** CLOSED 2026-04-24 ŌĆö 19ecf363 (fixed as part of S7-027 ŌĆö introduced localYmd() in ReportsPage). `packages/web/src/pages/reports/ReportsPage.tsx` line ~73. Fix: use `localYmd()` helper already defined in DashboardPage; lift to shared `packages/web/src/utils/date.ts`.

- [x] WEB-S7-032. **`ftsMatchExpr` in search.routes.ts strips all non-ASCII characters (regex `[^a-zA-Z0-9\s\-@.]`) ŌĆö searches for names with accents (caf├®, M├╝ller, ├æo├▒o) produce zero FTS tokens and silently fall through to LIKE.** CLOSED 2026-04-26 ŌĆö todofixes426: expanded character class to `├Ć-╔Å` (Latin + Latin Extended-A/B). `packages/server/src/routes/search.routes.ts`.

- [x] WEB-S7-033. **Inventory bulk price adjustment allows `priceAdjustPct` of 0 ŌĆö submits a no-op request that touches all selected rows unnecessarily, triggering audit log entries.** CLOSED 2026-04-24 ŌĆö 19ecf363 (fixed as part of S7-019). `packages/web/src/pages/inventory/InventoryListPage.tsx`. Fix: guard `if (pct === 0) { toast.error('Enter a non-zero adjustment'); return; }`.

- [x] WEB-S7-034. **Inline `isAdmin` check in search.routes.ts.** CLOSED 2026-04-26 ŌĆö todofixes426: added `isAdminOrManager(role)` helper + `ADMIN_MANAGER_ROLES` constant to `packages/server/src/utils/constants.ts`; both `isAdmin` checks in `search.routes.ts` updated to use the shared helper.

- [x] WEB-S7-035. **`TicketListPage` skeleton rows shown only after 150ms debounce (`showSkeleton`) ŌĆö fast responses cause a FOUT-like flicker where blank area appears then disappears; slow responses delay feedback.** `packages/web/src/pages/tickets/TicketListPage.tsx`. Fix: show skeleton immediately on `isLoading && !placeholderData`; remove the 150ms debounce or reduce to 0ms. FIXED-by-Fixer-A19 2026-04-25 ŌĆö `showSkeleton` effect now branches on `ticketData`: cold load (`isLoading && !ticketData`) sets the skeleton immediately so the user sees feedback within one frame; warm transitions (placeholderData hit) keep the 150ms debounce so the table doesn't jitter.

- [x] WEB-S7-036. **ReportsPage SalesTab empty chart.** CLOSED 2026-04-26 ŌĆö todofixes426: DONE-PREEXISTING ŌĆö `rows.length === 0` guard at line 316 already renders `<EmptyState message="No revenue data for this period" />` before the BarChart. `packages/web/src/pages/reports/ReportsPage.tsx`.

- [x] WEB-S7-037. **Portal timeline UTC-sort bug.** CLOSED 2026-04-26 ŌĆö todofixes426: DONE-PREEXISTING ŌĆö `portal.routes.ts` already has `toUtc` helper (appends 'Z' to naive timestamps) used in `timeline.sort()` at line 329. `packages/server/src/routes/portal.routes.ts`.

- [ ] WEB-S7-038. **`parsePage` returns 1 for page=0 or page=-1 (good) but also for page=99999 ŌĆö very large page numbers allowed server-side; sparse result sets return empty arrays silently with no "beyond last page" indicator.** `packages/server/src/utils/pagination.ts`. Fix: cap page at `Math.ceil(total / pageSize)` in route handlers and return `{ data: [], pagination: { ŌĆ” , out_of_bounds: true } }` so clients can redirect to last valid page.

- [x] WEB-S7-039. **Search global endpoint: `customers_fts` FTS exception is silently swallowed (`catch { }`) ŌĆö if FTS index is corrupt or missing, the catch block falls through to LIKE with no log entry, making the failure invisible.** `packages/server/src/routes/search.routes.ts` line 75 catch block. Fix: `catch (err) { logger.warn('FTS search failed, falling back to LIKE', { error: ŌĆ” }); }`. FIXED-by-Fixer-QQ 2026-04-25: replaced bare `catch {}` with `catch (err)` + `console.warn` carrying the error message so a busted FTS index surfaces in logs.


- [x] WEB-S7-041. **Dashboard "all" preset hardcoded floor.** CLOSED 2026-04-26 ŌĆö todofixes426: DONE-PREEXISTING ŌĆö `DashboardPage.tsx` `case 'all'` already uses `'2000-01-01'` not `'2020-01-01'`; RepairDesk data from 2018-2019 is covered. Server `GET /api/v1/reports/earliest-date` endpoint is a future enhancement if exact start date needed. `packages/web/src/pages/dashboard/DashboardPage.tsx`.

- [x] WEB-S7-042. **`GET /search/notes` minimum query length is 2 chars ŌĆö single-letter technician codes (e.g. "Z", "K" as author initials or part codes) return nothing; no user feedback on why.** CLOSED 2026-04-26 ŌĆö todofixes426: changed guard from `< 2` to `< 1`. `packages/server/src/routes/search.routes.ts`.

- [x] WEB-S7-043. **`portal_sessions` idle timeout evicts the session but does not clear the session cookie ŌĆö stale `portalToken` cookie keeps being sent on subsequent requests (always hitting 401) until browser expiry.** CLOSED 2026-04-26 ŌĆö todofixes426: `res.clearCookie('portalToken')` added before the 401 idle-timeout response. `packages/server/src/routes/portal.routes.ts`.

- [x] WEB-S7-044. **`enforceImportRateLimit` non-atomic prune+count.** CLOSED 2026-04-26 ŌĆö todofixes426: wrapped prune + all COUNT checks in a `db.transaction()` so the DELETE+SELECT chain is serialised; concurrent requests can no longer both see count=0 before either inserts. `packages/server/src/routes/import.routes.ts`.

- [x] WEB-S7-045. **ReportsPage CSV download detached anchor.** CLOSED 2026-04-26 ŌĆö todofixes426: DONE-PREEXISTING ŌĆö `downloadCsv` already does `document.body.appendChild(a); a.click();` and removes via `setTimeout` cleanup at lines 130-138. `packages/web/src/pages/reports/ReportsPage.tsx`.

---

### Severity summary (Wave S7, 45 findings)

P0 (critical ŌĆö data loss / silent failure / security): 8 findings (WEB-S7-001 through 008)
P1 (wrong data / significant UX failure / N+1 under load): 22 findings (WEB-S7-009 through 030)
P2 (edge case / minor inconsistency / cosmetic under specific conditions): 15 findings (WEB-S7-031 through 045)

Key patterns: (1) `isError` absent from 4 high-traffic list/detail pages ŌĆö silent blank screens on any API failure. (2) Hardcoded `$` + `.toFixed(2)` bypassing `formatCurrency()` in 3 pages. (3) No server-side date-format validation on filter inputs (SQLite silently returns NULL). (4) Naive date arithmetic ignores DST in reports and portal timeline sort. (5) `GET /inventory` missing `asyncHandler` ŌĆö process-crashing unhandled rejection.
### Dashboard Electron audit loop (2026-04-24+)

- [x] DASH-ELEC-001. **[HIGH][SEC] Token stored in process memory without expiry or clear cleanup path** ŌĆö packages/management/src/main/services/api-client.ts:204 ŌĆö `let superAdminToken: string | null = null` is module-level, persists until setSuperAdminToken(null) is called; on logout the token should be cleared AND revoked on the server before clearing locally; currently logout calls setSuperAdminToken(null) but no server revocation call observed; fix: add explicit token revocation POST before nullifying. PARTIAL-FIXED-by-Fixer-A28 2026-04-25 ŌĆö frontend/main-process side hardened with TTL self-eviction: api-client.ts now tracks `superAdminTokenSetAt` alongside the token, and the `getSuperAdminToken()` getter zeroes the slot when age exceeds the 12h cap (`SUPER_ADMIN_TOKEN_MAX_AGE_MS`). `apiRequest` now reads through the getter, so a long-idle main process whose renderer never called logout will hand back `null` on the next outbound authed call (server replies 401 ŌåÆ existing managementAuthExpired path drives the renderer to /login). Server-side revocation endpoint + pre-clear POST still pending (server work, out of frontend scope).

- [x] DASH-ELEC-002. **[HIGH][SEC] IPC handlers wrap exceptions with wrapHandler but don't guarantee main process doesn't crash on unhandled promise rejections** ŌĆö packages/management/src/main/ipc/management-api.ts:861 ŌĆö wrapHandler catches synchronous errors but an unhandled promise rejection inside apiRequest or concurrent async call will crash the main process; fix: add top-level process.on('unhandledRejection') handler in index.ts (one exists for uncaughtException but not unhandledRejection until line 124-126 which does handle it, but verify it returns gracefully and doesn't exit).

- [x] DASH-ELEC-003. **[MED][SEC] PowerShell script injection risk in spawnElevated via psQuote escaping** ŌĆö packages/management/src/main/index.ts:171 ŌĆö psQuote doubles single quotes but doesn't validate that `command` itself is a trusted literal; if a future maintainer adds variable input to `command` parameter (not just args) it will execute arbitrary code; fix: hardcode allowed commands in a Set at module top-level and reject any command not in the whitelist before spawning.

- [x] DASH-ELEC-004. **[MED][SEC] execSync in system-info.ts without timeout on PowerShell script inline string** ŌĆö packages/management/src/main/ipc/system-info.ts:158 ŌĆö the PowerShell script is hardcoded (safe) but passed as a string inside backticks; any future use of execSync with caller-supplied input will be vulnerable; fix: migrate all execSync calls to spawnSync with explicit argv array, or document the pattern so maintainers avoid inline shell strings.

- [x] DASH-ELEC-005. **[MED][WIRING] Service control IPC handlers don't validate that `state.root` in direct-server.json matches the trusted project root before using it** ŌĆö packages/management/src/main/ipc/service-control.ts:303-320 ŌĆö readDirectState() calls isProjectRoot(parsed.root) but isProjectRoot only checks for package.json markers, not that the path matches resolveTrustedProjectRoot(); AUDIT-MGT-030 comment acknowledges this but the cross-check should happen BEFORE the function returns; currently a typo in the PID file's `root` field that still has package.json would be accepted; fix: move the trustedRoot check inside readDirectState before returning.

- [x] DASH-ELEC-006. **[LOW][WIRING] IPC handlers for env-settings (admin:get-env-settings, admin:set-env-settings) don't appear to validate against SERVER_ENV_ALLOWLIST at handler boundary** ŌĆö packages/management/src/main/ipc/management-api.ts ŌĆö grep shows handlers exist but detailed validation not found in the audit scope; fix: verify both GET and SET envelope the .env keys through the allowlist at IPC layer, not just inside the server's env-startup code.

- [ ] DASH-ELEC-007. **[LOW][SEC] No rate-limit or request-deduplication on IPC invoke calls from renderer** ŌĆö packages/management/src/preload/index.ts:117-125 ŌĆö safeInvoke passes through to ipcRenderer.invoke() with no dedup or throttling; a rapid-fire loop calling `management.getStats()` 1000 times will spawn 1000 API requests; fix: add optional debounce/throttle wrapper on hot-path invokes (stats, disk-space polling).

- [x] DASH-ELEC-008. **[LOW][WIRING] vite.config.ts has sourcemap disabled for prod but no explicit mention of dev-sourcemaps handling** ŌĆö packages/management/src/main/vite.config.ts:17 ŌĆö `sourcemap: false` is set but dev mode sourcemaps aren't explicitly configured; if dev build is packaged accidentally with sourcemap enabled, renderer code is exposed; fix: add explicit `sourcemap: false` comment or conditional logic to ensure dev builds are never packaged with sourcemaps.

- [x] DASH-ELEC-009. **[LOW][SEC] updateBrowserWindow error paths in management-api.ts don't surface error detail on failure** ŌĆö packages/management/src/main/ipc/management-api.ts (lines ~1400+) ŌĆö git fetch/checkout/verify failures are swallowed in the error case and return a generic "update check failed" message; attacker who poisons git binary or redirects origin sees no diagnostics; fix: log full spawnSync result (stderr) to main process logs so operators can diagnose update failures without user visibility to the command itself.

- [ ] DASH-ELEC-010. **[LOW][WIRING] No explicit audit log of IPC calls that modify system state (restart, stop, create-tenant, delete-tenant)** ŌĆö all of packages/management/src/main/ipc/*.ts ŌĆö sensitive operations like `service:restart`, `super-admin:delete-tenant` succeed silently without recording in a main-process audit log who (which renderer origin) initiated them; fix: add a per-file audit logger that records timestamp, origin, operation, and result to a rotating audit.log alongside dashboard.log for compliance/forensics.


- [x] DASH-ELEC-011. **[MED][WIRING] RecentActivityWidget and DiagnosticsPage use manual `cancelled` flag instead of AbortController for fetch cleanup** ŌĆö packages/management/src/renderer/src/components/RecentActivityWidget.tsx:39-59, packages/management/src/renderer/src/pages/DiagnosticsPage.tsx:40-53 ŌĆö Promise.all() responses are checked against a cancelled boolean on unmount, but if a response arrives AFTER unmount but BEFORE the flag is checked, the state-setter will still fire and cause a memory leak warning; fix: replace with AbortController so the actual fetch is terminated, not just the state update.

- [x] DASH-ELEC-012. **[MED][WIRING] useServerHealth hook lacks AbortSignal for concurrent getStats + service.getStatus calls** ŌĆö packages/management/src/renderer/src/hooks/useServerHealth.ts:46-51 ŌĆö Promise.all([api.management.getStats(), api.service.getStatus()]) has no abort signal, so if the user logs out mid-poll the pending requests continue and may trigger an update to a dead store; fix: add AbortController at hook level and pass signal to both IPC calls (if the IPC bridge supports it).

- [ ] DASH-ELEC-013. **[MED][WIRING] QueryClient staleTime=10s but no explicit refetchInterval or polling strategy in management pages** ŌĆö packages/management/src/renderer/src/main.tsx:60-68 ŌĆö TanStack Query is configured but pages use manual setInterval (useInterval hook, useServerHealth setTimeout) instead of useQuery; mixed polling strategies may cause redundant fetches; fix: migrate high-frequency polls (stats, crashes, audit log) to useQuery with refetchInterval so react-query deduplicates and batches requests.

- [x] DASH-ELEC-014. **[LOW][WIRING] CrashMonitorPage refreshes on interval (30s) but polls are not cancelled on page unmount** ŌĆö packages/management/src/renderer/src/pages/CrashMonitorPage.tsx:45-49 ŌĆö setInterval(refresh, 30_000) is cleaned up correctly, but refresh() calls do not use AbortController; fix: add AbortController to CrashMonitorPage's refresh so pending Promise.all responses don't setState after unmount. ŌĆö Fixer-C18 2026-04-25: mountedRef guard added; refresh() short-circuits all setState after unmount so in-flight Promise.all resolves into the void without warnings.

- [ ] DASH-ELEC-015. **[MED][WIRING] No error boundary wrapping individual page content, only top-level and PageErrorBoundary** ŌĆö packages/management/src/renderer/src/components/layout/DashboardShell.tsx:30-32 ŌĆö PageErrorBoundary wraps Outlet but a render error in Header, Sidebar, StatusFooter, or Banner components will crash the entire shell; fix: split PageErrorBoundary into smaller boundaries per major layout section (header, sidebar, main, footer).

- [x] DASH-ELEC-016. **[LOW][WIRING] CSV export in AuditLogPage and CrashMonitorPage doesn't check for toCsv injection risk with special leading characters** ŌĆö packages/management/src/renderer/src/utils/csv.ts:13-20 ŌĆö escapeCsvField wraps fields with quotes if they contain comma/quote/newline, but RFC-4180 sec.2 note 2 recommends quoting fields starting with =, +, @, - to prevent spreadsheet formula injection; fix: add check in escapeCsvField to prepend single quote if s[0] matches /[=+@-]/.

## Web Audit Wave-WEB-2026-04-24 Search S8 ŌĆö RBAC + backend route gaps


- [x] WEB-S8-002. CLOSED 2026-04-26 ŌĆö todofixes426. **`GET /api/v1/import/repairdesk/status` and `GET /api/v1/import/history` have no role check ŌĆö any authenticated user (technician, cashier) can read all import run history, including error logs that may contain sensitive API-response fragments.** `packages/server/src/routes/import.routes.ts` lines 346, 436. Fix: add `if (req.user?.role !== 'admin') throw new AppError(ŌĆ”, 403)` at the top of both handlers, identical to the guard on `/start` (line 230).

- [x] WEB-S8-003. CLOSED 2026-04-26 ŌĆö todofixes426. **`GET /api/v1/import/repairshopr/status` and `GET /api/v1/import/myrepairapp/status` same gap as WEB-S8-002.** `packages/server/src/routes/import.routes.ts` lines 722, 1052. Fix: add admin role gate matching `/repairdesk/status`.





- [x] WEB-S8-008. CLOSED 2026-04-26 ŌĆö todofixes426. **`GET /api/v1/tickets/tv-display` (inside `tickets.routes.ts`, served under `authMiddleware`) returns `customer_first_name` and `assigned_tech` full name ŌĆö the data that `tv.routes.ts` deliberately redacted for the unauthenticated TV endpoint is re-exposed here to any authenticated role.** `packages/server/src/routes/tickets.routes.ts` lines 1632ŌĆō1664. Fix: restricted to `requireAdminOrManager` (option a).








- [x] WEB-S8-016. CLOSED 2026-04-26 ŌĆö todofixes426. **`GET /api/v1/reports/presets`, `POST /api/v1/reports/presets`, `PUT /api/v1/reports/presets/:presetId`, `DELETE /api/v1/reports/presets/:presetId` ŌĆö no role check beyond `authMiddleware`. Any user can create/read/update/delete report presets. The PUT and DELETE check `user_id = req.user.id` ownership correctly, but GET lists all presets for the current user regardless of role ŌĆö a cashier saving presets for financial reports they cannot see is a UX inconsistency.** `packages/server/src/routes/reports.routes.ts` lines 1471ŌĆō1600. Fix: `requireAdminOrManager` added to all four preset handlers.


- [x] WEB-S8-018. CLOSED 2026-04-25 ŌĆö f7781356. **`GET /api/v1/roles/permission-keys` has no auth check beyond the global `authMiddleware` ŌĆö any authenticated user can retrieve the full list of permission key strings.** `packages/server/src/routes/roles.routes.ts` line 116. Low sensitivity (no values, just names) but unnecessarily exposed. Fix: add `requireAdmin(req)` to match all sibling routes.

- [x] WEB-S8-019. CLOSED 2026-04-25 ŌĆö f7781356. **`GET /api/v1/roles/users/:userId/role` has no role check ŌĆö any authenticated user can look up the custom role assignment for any user ID (enumeration of role assignments).** `packages/server/src/routes/roles.routes.ts` line 336. Fix: add `requireAdmin(req)`.

- [x] WEB-S8-020. CLOSED 2026-04-25 ŌĆö 7a5d4da8. **`GET /api/v1/settings/config` returns all `store_config` rows to any authenticated user; only `SENSITIVE_CONFIG_KEYS` are filtered for non-admins. But the key set may evolve ŌĆö new sensitive keys added to the DB without being added to `SENSITIVE_CONFIG_KEYS` silently leak to all staff.** `packages/server/src/routes/settings.routes.ts` line 337. Fix: invert the model ŌĆö maintain a `PUBLIC_CONFIG_KEYS` allowlist (e.g. `store_name`, `currency`, `timezone`) and return only those to non-admins instead of filtering a denylist.

- [x] WEB-S8-021. CLOSED 2026-04-25 ŌĆö 7a5d4da8. **`GET /api/v1/settings/preferences` and `PUT /api/v1/settings/preferences` ŌĆö no `asyncHandler` wrapping; both use plain `async (req, res)` directly. An unhandled rejection crashes the worker process.** `packages/server/src/routes/settings.routes.ts` lines 1946, 1959. Fix: wrap both with `asyncHandler(ŌĆ”)`.

- [x] WEB-S8-022. CLOSED 2026-04-25 ŌĆö 7a5d4da8. **`GET /api/v1/settings/setup-status`, `GET /api/v1/settings/store`, `GET /api/v1/settings/statuses`, `GET /api/v1/settings/tax-classes`, `GET /api/v1/settings/payment-methods`, `GET /api/v1/settings/referral-sources`, `GET /api/v1/settings/customer-groups` ŌĆö all read-only settings endpoints use plain `async (req, res)` without `asyncHandler`. Thrown DB errors cause unhandled promise rejections that crash Express.** `packages/server/src/routes/settings.routes.ts` lines 270, 517, 563, 688, 799, 816, 833. Fix: wrap all handlers with `asyncHandler`.

- [x] WEB-S8-023. CLOSED 2026-04-25 ŌĆö 7a5d4da8. **`GET /api/v1/settings/module-visibility` uses plain `async (req, res)` without `asyncHandler`.** `packages/server/src/routes/settings.routes.ts` line 2004. Fix: wrap with `asyncHandler`.

- [x] WEB-S8-024. CLOSED 2026-04-25 ŌĆö e3321a6e. **`GET /api/v1/sms/templates` ŌĆö reads all SMS templates with no role check (any authenticated user).** `packages/server/src/routes/sms.routes.ts` line 850. Templates contain canned response text that may reveal internal escalation paths or customer-service scripts. Fix: add `requireManagerOrAdmin(req)` to match the write sibling handlers.

- [x] WEB-S8-025. Fix: add role gate and bound `vars` object (max 20 keys, each key/value Ōēż 200 chars).



- [x] WEB-S8-028. CLOSED 2026-04-24 ŌĆö 18a2d442. **`GET /api/v1/catalog/order-queue` leaks `customer` first+last name and `order_id` of the associated ticket via the `tickets_json` JOIN ŌĆö any technician with auth can enumerate which customers have parts on order.** `packages/server/src/routes/catalog.routes.ts` lines 607ŌĆō649. - [x] WEB-S8-029. CLOSED 2026-04-25 ŌĆö f7781356. **`POST /api/v1/import/myrepairapp/nuclear` validates password re-entry but the `confirm` field check (`confirm !== 'NUCLEAR'`) runs BEFORE the role check ŌĆö a non-admin can probe whether the endpoint exists by omitting `confirm` and getting a 400 (not 403). Minor information leak.** `packages/server/src/routes/import.routes.ts` lines 1135ŌĆō1154. Fix: move the role check to line 1 of the handler, before any other validation.

- [x] WEB-S8-030. - [x] WEB-S8-031. - [x] WEB-S8-034. - [x] WEB-S8-035. Fix: add `requirePermission('inventory.view')` as middleware arg before `asyncHandler`.

- [x] WEB-S8-036. CLOSED 2026-04-24 ŌĆö e3321a6e. **Rate limiting missing on `POST /api/v1/catalog/live-search` ŌĆö each call triggers an outbound HTTP scrape against a supplier site. No per-user, no per-tenant, no global cap.** `packages/server/src/routes/catalog.routes.ts` line 587. A single compromised JWT can generate unbounded scrape traffic. Fix: add `consumeWindowRate(req.db, 'catalog_live_search', String(req.user!.id), 10, 60_000)`.

- [x] WEB-S8-037. CLOSED 2026-04-26 ŌĆö todofixes426. **`POST /api/v1/catalog/sync` (trigger supplier catalog scrape) has `adminOnly` guard but no rate limit ŌĆö an admin session can fire unlimited scrape jobs back-to-back (there is a per-source in-progress lock, but a rapid retry loop floods the `scrape_jobs` table with failed rows).** `packages/server/src/routes/catalog.routes.ts` line 230. Fix: `consumeWindowRate(req.db, 'catalog_sync', String(req.user!.id), 3, 3_600_000)` added (3 per hour per admin).

- [x] WEB-S8-038. CLOSED 2026-04-25 ŌĆö 7a5d4da8. **`GET /api/v1/settings/audit-logs` uses plain `async (req, res)` without `asyncHandler` ŌĆö all other `adminOnly` handlers in settings use plain async too.** `packages/server/src/routes/settings.routes.ts` line 1807. Covered by a broader pattern; the audit-log endpoint is especially important. Fix: wrap with `asyncHandler`.

- [x] WEB-S8-039. CLOSED 2026-04-24 ŌĆö 6ea75e92. **Multi-tenant: `GET /api/v1/import/repairdesk/status` (and RS/MRA equivalents) include checkpoint data keyed by `tenantSlug` but use `req.asyncDb` (already tenant-scoped). If the slug resolution fails silently and falls back to `'default'`, checkpoint data from another tenant leaks.** `packages/server/src/routes/import.routes.ts` line 384: `const tenantSlug = (req as any).tenantSlug || 'default'`. Fix: reject with 500 if `req.tenantSlug` is undefined in multi-tenant mode rather than falling back to a shared key.

- [x] WEB-S8-040. CLOSED 2026-04-24 ŌĆö 18a2d442. **`GET /api/v1/employees/performance/all` returns `total_revenue` (sum of ticket totals per tech) to any authenticated user ŌĆö this is financial data.** `packages/server/src/routes/employees.routes.ts` line 195. Fix: add `requireAdminOrManager` gate.

- [x] WEB-S8-041. CLOSED 2026-04-25 ŌĆö 7a5d4da8. **`settings.routes.ts` wide pattern: at least 15 read-only endpoints (statuses, tax-classes, payment-methods, referral-sources, customer-groups, notification-templates, checklist-templates, condition-templates, condition-checks, receipt-templates, webhook-events-enum, sms-providers) use raw `async (req, res)` without `asyncHandler`. An unhandled rejection from any DB call crashes the request thread without an error response.** `packages/server/src/routes/settings.routes.ts` (multiple lines throughout the file). Fix: global search for `async (req, res)` in settings.routes.ts and wrap all with `asyncHandler`.

- [x] WEB-S8-042. CLOSED 2026-04-24 ŌĆö e3321a6e. **`POST /api/v1/sms/send` records a rate-limit failure on every successful send (`recordWindowFailure` is called unconditionally after the rate check passes) ŌĆö this means after 5 sends in 60 s, the 6th send is blocked even if the window counter was correct before the extra increment.** `packages/server/src/routes/sms.routes.ts` line 499: `recordWindowFailure(req.db, 'sms_send', rateLimitKey, 60000)` called on non-failure path. Fix: rename/replace with `recordWindowAttempt` (which doesn't penalize the counter double), or use the atomic `consumeWindowRate` helper.

- [x] WEB-S8-043. CLOSED 2026-04-24 ŌĆö 18a2d442. **`GET /api/v1/team/shifts` in `team.routes.ts` (line 83) queries all shifts for all users when no `user_id` filter is given ŌĆö a manager-or-admin check is absent for the "list all" path, exposing every employee's full shift schedule to any authenticated user.** `packages/server/src/routes/team.routes.ts` lines 83ŌĆō113. Fix: require `requireAdminOrManager` when `user_id` is absent (all-users query) and clamp to self for non-privileged callers.

- [x] WEB-S8-044. CLOSED 2026-04-24 ŌĆö 18a2d442. **`GET /api/v1/inventory/` returns `cost_price` in every inventory row to any authenticated user ŌĆö cost price is margin-sensitive data that cashiers/technicians should not see.** `packages/server/src/routes/inventory.routes.ts` line 64. Fix: either add `requirePermission('inventory.view')` (which admin/manager roles hold) or project the response to omit `cost_price` for non-privileged roles.

- [ ] WEB-S8-045. **`settings.routes.ts` `GET /settings/users` is gated with `adminOnly` but the returned row shape includes `role` and `is_active` for all users ŌĆö acceptable. However `PUT /settings/users/:id` (line 962) validates the new `role` against `VALID_ROLES` allowlist but also accepts `permissions` as a raw JSON blob from `req.body`, allowing any admin to write arbitrary permission overrides without schema validation or audit logging.** `packages/server/src/routes/settings.routes.ts` line 962+. Fix: parse and validate `permissions` against `VALID_PERMISSIONS` allowlist keys before storing; write an audit row for every permission change identical to the role-change audit.

---

### Severity summary (Wave S8, 45 findings)

P0 (critical ŌĆö privilege escalation / unauthenticated mutation / process crash): 5 findings (WEB-S8-001, WEB-S8-004, WEB-S8-006, WEB-S8-010, WEB-S8-042)
P1 (missing role gate on sensitive data / IDOR / missing rate limit on expensive operations): 27 findings (WEB-S8-002 through WEB-S8-009, WEB-S8-011 through WEB-S8-017, WEB-S8-019 through WEB-S8-022, WEB-S8-024 through WEB-S8-031, WEB-S8-034 through WEB-S8-040, WEB-S8-043 through WEB-S8-044)
P2 (information disclosure / minor inconsistency / defense-in-depth): 13 findings (WEB-S8-018, WEB-S8-023, WEB-S8-028, WEB-S8-029, WEB-S8-032 through WEB-S8-033, WEB-S8-041, WEB-S8-045)

Key patterns: (1) Systemic absence of `requirePermission` on read-only inventory, catalog, and employee endpoints ŌĆö cost prices, supplier data, and employee revenue visible to any role. (2) `import.routes.ts` status/history endpoints lack admin gate matching their sibling start/cancel endpoints. (3) `settings.routes.ts` uses raw `async (req, res)` throughout ŌĆö ~15 handlers missing `asyncHandler`, creating unhandled-rejection crash vectors. (4) `catalog.routes.ts` import and live-search endpoints are ungated mutations that any authenticated user can call. (5) Tenant-isolation fallback to `'default'` slug in import checkpoints risks cross-tenant data exposure in multi-tenant mode.
### Wave-Loop Finder-I run 2026-04-24 ŌĆö api/routing/hooks/stores deeper-pass

- [x] WEB-FI-001. **[HIGH] axios `client` has no request `timeout` ŌĆö long-tail backend stalls hang fetches forever, leaking spinners + react-query promises across tab lifetime.** `api/client.ts:42-46` only sets `baseURL` + `withCredentials`; the public signup client correctly sets `timeout: 15_000` (endpoints.ts:1207) but the authenticated client doesn't. A slow upstream (DB lock, blocked event loop) keeps the request pending; React Query never errors out, error boundaries never trigger, the user sees a forever-spinner. Add `timeout: 30_000` (or per-route override) so failures surface as ECONNABORTED within a bounded window. FIXED 2026-04-24 by Fixer-H ŌĆö added `DEFAULT_REQUEST_TIMEOUT_MS = 30_000` constant to `packages/web/src/api/client.ts` and wired it into `axios.create` for the authenticated client; per-route callers can still override via `client.post(url, body, { timeout: 60_000 })` for uploads/exports.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/api; files=packages/web/src/api/client.ts:42-46; fix=add-default-timeout+per-route-override -->

- [x] WEB-FI-002. **[HIGH] `superAdminClient` lacks `withCredentials` AND has no timeout ŌĆö super-admin session bearer is the only auth surface, and every call can stall indefinitely.** `client.ts:301-304`: bare `axios.create({ baseURL: '/super-admin/api', headers: ... })`. No `withCredentials`, no `timeout`. A super-admin tenant impersonation that hangs leaves the operator stuck staring at the spinner; the bearer is the only credential so the SA console has no graceful degradation. Add `timeout: 30_000` and decide explicitly whether SA also wants cookies. FIXED-by-Fixer-ZZ 2026-04-25 ŌĆö added `timeout: 30_000` to `superAdminClient` `axios.create` matching the tenant client. `withCredentials` left off (SA bearer is the only credential ŌĆö explicit decision noted in the inline comment).
  <!-- meta: scope=web/api; files=packages/web/src/api/client.ts:301-335; fix=add-timeout+document-withCredentials-policy -->

- [x] WEB-FI-003. **[HIGH] `client.ts` 401-handler retries the original request once via `_retry` but if the retried request still 401s the response is rejected to the caller WITHOUT a logout ŌĆö the auth store still thinks the user is authenticated.** `client.ts:261-271`. If the new access token is rejected by the server (clock skew, token-version bump, role change between issuance and use), the second 401 falls through to the caller and the user keeps seeing 401 toasts on every action. Add a fallback: if the retried request still 401s, call `forceLogout('session-expired')`. FIXED 2026-04-24 by Fixer-H ŌĆö wrapped the post-refresh `client(originalRequest)` retry in its own try/catch in `packages/web/src/api/client.ts`; on a second 401 the handler now calls `forceLogout('session-expired')` and rejects the caller. The retry-error status is read via a typed-narrow access (no `any` cast).
  <!-- meta: scope=web/api; files=packages/web/src/api/client.ts:261-271; fix=on-second-401-call-forceLogout-and-suppress-toast -->

- [x] WEB-FI-004. **[HIGH] `client.ts` 5xx auto-toast (line 278-284) fires for EVERY failed mutation including ones with their own `onError` UI ŌĆö dual toasts on each server error.** Components using `useMutation({ onError: (err) => toast.error(formatApiError(err)) })` already display a toast; the response interceptor unconditionally fires `toast.error('Server error...')` first. User sees two toasts stacked, or worse, a generic "Server error" that overrides a specific server message. Add an opt-out (e.g. `config.skipGlobal500Toast`) or convert to event-bus + opt-in instead. FIXED-by-Fixer-ZZ 2026-04-25 ŌĆö interceptor now reads `originalRequest.skipGlobal500Toast === true` and short-circuits the global `toast.error` for that request. Default behavior preserved (existing callers unchanged); opting in is `client.post(url, body, { skipGlobal500Toast: true })`.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/api; files=packages/web/src/api/client.ts:278-284; fix=add-opt-out-flag-or-emit-event-instead-of-toast -->

- [x] WEB-FI-005 / FIXED-by-Fixer-A11 2026-04-25. **[HIGH] `LOGOUT_REQUIRED_EVENT` listener in `authStore.ts:143` does `window.location.href = '/login'` which throws away the React tree, in-flight uploads, unsaved drafts.** Hard nav defeats `useDraft` (debounced `setTimeout` saves discarded mid-write ŌĆö losing up to 2s of typed text), pending photo uploads, in-flight WS messages. SPA-internal `Navigate` would preserve drafts and let `auth-cleared` fire to clean up state cleanly. Switch to `react-router` navigation guarded by a "discard or save" prompt for dirty forms.
  FIXED-by-Fixer-A11 2026-04-25 ŌĆö both `window.location.href = '/login'` sites in `stores/authStore.ts` (cross-tab storage handler + `LOGOUT_REQUIRED_EVENT` listener) now dispatch a new `bizarre-crm:request-login-nav` event. `App.tsx` mounts a router-aware bridge that consumes the event and calls `navigate('/login', { replace: true })` so the React tree, useDraft beforeunload flush, and WS teardown all run before the route changes. A `__bizarreLoginNavReady` flag + 0 ms `setTimeout` fallback in authStore preserves the old hard-nav behavior in the corner case where App hasn't mounted yet (e.g. cold-start crash inside Suspense), so no path can deadlock on a stale protected page.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/stores; files=packages/web/src/stores/authStore.ts,packages/web/src/App.tsx; fix=use-router-navigate-not-window.location.href -->

- [x] WEB-FI-006. **[MED] `axios.post` for refresh in `performRefresh` calls the BARE `axios` (not the configured `client`), so it never picks up the client default timeout ŌĆö and crucially has NO timeout of its own.** `client.ts:65-69`: `axios.post(AUTH_REFRESH_URL, {}, { withCredentials, headers })`. A refresh that hangs forever (DNS, slow auth service, network dropout) prevents the 401 retry from EVER resolving ŌĆö every queued request waits on `sharedRefreshPromise` which never settles. Add an explicit `timeout: 10_000` and reject the slot on timeout so callers fail fast. FIXED-by-Fixer-B6 2026-04-25 ŌĆö added `timeout: 10_000` to the bare `axios.post(AUTH_REFRESH_URL, ŌĆ”)` in `performRefresh`. The promise now rejects after 10s instead of hanging, so the `finally` clears `sharedRefreshPromise` and queued 401 retries fail fast (and trigger logout) rather than wedging the whole client.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/api; files=packages/web/src/api/client.ts:58-80; fix=add-explicit-timeout-on-refresh-axios.post -->

- [x] WEB-FI-007. **[MED] `App.tsx` `ProtectedRoute` does not preserve the user's intended path on redirect ŌĆö `Navigate to="/login"` drops `from`, so post-login users always land on `/` instead of the deep link they tried to open.** Lines 141. Standard React Router pattern is `<Navigate to="/login" state={{ from: location }} replace />` and the LoginPage reads `location.state?.from?.pathname` after success. Without it, every email-link / bookmarked deep link bounces to dashboard after re-login. (Note: passing `from` via state ŌĆö NOT a query string ŌĆö also avoids the `?from=` XSS angle the audit guidelines warn about.) ŌĆö Fixer-FFF 2026-04-25: ProtectedRoute now passes `state={{ from: location }}`; LoginPage derives a guarded `fromPath` (rejects non-`/`-prefixed and `//`-prefixed values to block off-origin redirect) and uses it in all three post-auth `navigate()` calls (already-auth check, auto-login via `/me`, 2FA verify).
  <!-- meta: scope=web/routing; files=packages/web/src/App.tsx:141; fix=Navigate-with-state.from+LoginPage-redirect-after-login -->

- [x] WEB-FI-008. **[MED] `App.tsx` `SuperAdminRoute` reads `localStorage.getItem(SUPER_ADMIN_TOKEN_KEY)` once at component-render time but never re-checks ŌĆö if the token is removed by the response interceptor (401/403), the rendered page stays mounted until the next route navigation.** Lines 184. The component only re-renders when its parent does; revoking SA via the interceptor's `removeItem` doesn't trigger a re-mount. Either subscribe to `SUPER_ADMIN_LOGOUT_EVENT` and force a re-render, or subscribe to the storage event so other tabs also propagate the logout.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/routing; files=packages/web/src/App.tsx:183-198; fix=subscribe-SUPER_ADMIN_LOGOUT_EVENT-or-storage-listener -->

- [x] WEB-FI-009. **[MED] `main.tsx` global `unhandledrejection` + `error` listeners trigger a hard `window.location.reload()` on any chunk-load error pattern ŌĆö but the regex is over-broad, matching any user-thrown error containing phrases like "module script".** Lines 122-126,158-170. A user-defined error message with that substring would trigger an infinite-reload loop limited only by the 30-second sentinel. Tighten the predicate to also require `name === 'TypeError'` since real chunk-load failures always surface as TypeError. ŌĆö Fixer-SSS 2026-04-25.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/root; files=packages/web/src/main.tsx:122-170; fix=narrow-predicate-to-TypeError+regex-only -->

- [x] WEB-FI-010. **[MED] `useWebSocket` invalidation map calls `queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: qk.filter((k) => k !== undefined) })` ŌĆö `undefined` slots are pruned, but that means a key like `['ticket', undefined]` becomes `['ticket']`, which under tanstack v5 invalidates EVERY query starting with `['ticket']`.** `useWebSocket.ts:277`. Intent is "if id is unknown skip the partial key", actual effect is "match all". When the server sends a `ticket:status_changed` event with a missing id, this re-fetches the ENTIRE ticket subtree across every page. Drop the entry entirely if any required slot is undefined. ŌĆö Fixer-SSS 2026-04-25.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/hooks; files=packages/web/src/hooks/useWebSocket.ts:273-296; fix=skip-invalidation-if-required-slot-missing -->

- [x] WEB-FI-011. **[MED] `useWebSocket` reads the access token in `connect()` and sends it in the `onopen` `auth` message ŌĆö a token rotated by `performRefresh` between `connect()` and `onopen` firing is captured stale, server rejects with 4001.** `useWebSocket.ts:226,246-249`. Common during 401 burst recovery. Re-read `localStorage.getItem('accessToken')` inside `ws.onopen` immediately before sending so the freshest token wins. ŌĆö Fixer-SSS 2026-04-25.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/hooks; files=packages/web/src/hooks/useWebSocket.ts:246-249; fix=re-read-localStorage-inside-ws.onopen -->

- [ ] WEB-FI-012. **[MED] `usePosKeyboardShortcuts` swallows F-keys with `event.preventDefault()` ŌĆö handlers are read via `handlersRef.current` but if a parent's handler closure captured stale state and is updated only on commit, the F-key fires the previous-render value.** `usePosKeyboardShortcuts.ts:46-74`. Documenting handlers as "must read fresh state via refs/store" is a footgun. Either pass fresh args via a callback registry or document this prominently in the hook header.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/hooks; files=packages/web/src/hooks/usePosKeyboardShortcuts.ts:46-74; fix=document-stale-closure-risk+example-using-store -->

- [x] WEB-FI-013. **[MED] `useDraft` writes to `localStorage` with no per-tenant prefix ŌĆö drafts written under tenant A are visible to tenant B if the same browser logs into a second tenant on the same origin.** `useDraft.ts:36-48`: keys are caller-supplied (e.g. `'ticket-1234-notes'`) with no tenant scoping. Customer notes / private comments persisted as drafts will leak across tenant logins on the same machine. Either prefix all draft keys with the tenant slug at hook-call sites, or have `useDraft` itself read tenant from `useAuthStore` and prefix automatically. FIXED 2026-04-24 by Fixer-H ŌĆö `packages/web/src/hooks/useDraft.ts` now resolves every caller-supplied key through `buildScopedKey()` which prefixes `bizarrecrm:draft:<userId>:` (or `bizarrecrm:draft:anon:` when the auth store has not hydrated). Mount, debounced save, and `clearDraft` all use the scoped key; the schedule-time capture (SCAN-601) is preserved via a `scopedKeyRef`.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/hooks; files=packages/web/src/hooks/useDraft.ts:36-94; fix=prefix-key-with-tenant.slug+wipe-on-auth-cleared -->

- [x] WEB-FI-014. **[MED] `useDraft` does not subscribe to `bizarre-crm:auth-cleared` ŌĆö drafts persist in `localStorage` across logout, exposing the previous user's text on the next sign-in.** Same file as FI-013. The `auth-cleared` listeners in main.tsx + planStore wipe React Query + plan state but `localStorage` draft keys survive. A shared kiosk where Alice writes a sensitive customer note, logs out, Bob logs in ŌĆö Bob's first visit to the same form restores Alice's draft. Add an `auth-cleared` listener that wipes all keys matching a known draft prefix. FIXED 2026-04-24 by Fixer-H ŌĆö module-level `addEventListener('bizarre-crm:auth-cleared', wipeAllDrafts)` in `packages/web/src/hooks/useDraft.ts` walks `localStorage` and removes every key matching `^bizarrecrm:draft:`. Runs once on module load, behaves consistently for both mounted and unmounted draft instances, and survives logout / forced-logout / switch-user since all three flows emit `auth-cleared`.

- [x] WEB-FG-001. **[HIGH] Super-admin JWT stored in `localStorage` is XSS-exfiltratable; one stored-XSS anywhere on the surface yields full cross-tenant impersonation.** `TenantsListPage.tsx:67,251,312` write/read `SUPER_ADMIN_TOKEN_KEY` with `localStorage.setItem/getItem/removeItem`. Token bears the `impersonate(slug)` privilege ŌĆö a single XSS payload can iterate every tenant + provision a logged-in session for each. Also no `expiresAt` check on read; an expired but un-purged token still flips `isAuthenticated=true` for one render. Closes the "expired-but-not-yet-purged token flips `isAuthenticated=true` for one render" race; signature verification stays server-side.

- [x] WEB-FG-014. **[MED] `StepLogo` upload accepts any file the user picks ŌĆö `accept="image/jpeg,image/png,image/webp,image/gif"` is a hint, not a guard, and the dropper has no MIME re-check before posting `multipart/form-data`.** `StepLogo.tsx:22-53`. ### Wave-Loop Finder-H run 2026-04-24 ŌĆö pos/catalog/inventory deeper-pass

- [x] WEB-FH-001. **[HIGH] POS checkout has NO idempotency key ŌĆö double-click "Complete Checkout" can charge twice.** `posApi.checkoutWithTicket` (`packages/web/src/api/endpoints.ts:600`) is a bare `api.post('/pos/checkout-with-ticket', data)` with no `X-Idempotency-Key` header, while sibling `invoiceApi.create` + `recordPayment` (lines 249-265) DO send one. The "Complete Checkout" button in `CheckoutModal.tsx:656-663` is only client-side debounced via `processing` state ŌĆö a slow 5-10s server response with a flaky network re-try (browser auto-retry, user backgrounding+foregrounding the tab, or a quick second click before `setProcessing(true)` paints) creates two invoices + double-charges the customer's card. POS endpoint is the single highest-stakes mutation in the app. FIXED 2026-04-24 by Fixer-G ŌĆö `posApi.checkoutWithTicket` now sends `X-Idempotency-Key`; key is minted ONCE per cart-session in the unified-pos store (`ensureIdempotencyKey`), persisted across page-refresh, reused by both CheckoutModal + BottomActions create-ticket path, dropped on `clearCart` / `resetAll`.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/api+web/pages/unified-pos; files=packages/web/src/api/endpoints.ts:600,packages/web/src/pages/unified-pos/CheckoutModal.tsx:318-382; fix=add-X-Idempotency-Key-header-on-checkoutWithTicket+per-modal-uuid-stable-across-retries -->

- [x] WEB-FH-002. **[HIGH] Existing idempotency-key generator runs INSIDE the api function ŌĆö every call (including retries) mints a fresh UUID, defeating the cache.** Pattern at `endpoints.ts:252-254` calls `globalThis.crypto?.randomUUID()` inside the `create` function body. If the user double-clicks, the second call generates a different key and the server sees two distinct requests. The idempotent middleware caches by `(user,url,key)` so the second call is processed as new. Same gap on `recordPayment` line 263. The "DA-6" comment claim is incorrect ŌĆö keys must be stable across retries (form-scoped, not call-scoped). FIXED 2026-04-24 by Fixer-G ŌĆö `invoiceApi.create`, `invoiceApi.recordPayment`, and `posApi.checkoutWithTicket` now accept an optional `idempotencyKey` argument that callers mint ONCE at form-open / cart-create and pass on every retry; internal mint kept only as a fallback for legacy callers until they migrate.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/api; files=packages/web/src/api/endpoints.ts:246-265; fix=accept-key-as-arg-and-mint-once-per-form-submit-then-pass-on-retries -->

- [x] WEB-FH-003. **[HIGH] LeftPanel Enter+Click race fires `addProduct` twice for the same item.** `UnifiedSearchBar` has both `onKeyDown(e.key==='Enter') -> results[0].action()` (line 196-200) AND each result's `onMouseDown(e.preventDefault(); r.action())` (line 211). Pressing Enter while clicking the first result OR scanning a barcode that emits Enter+chars fires `addProduct` twice ŌĆö cart shows qty=2. Same hazard in `BarcodeSearch.handleKey` (line 343-370): no in-flight guard, so two rapid scanner emissions both call `posApi.products` + `addProduct`. Compounds the no-idempotency issue. FIXED 2026-04-24 by Fixer-G ŌĆö added `actionInFlightRef` + `fireOnce()` wrapper in `UnifiedSearchBar` (250 ms cooldown applied symmetrically on Enter-keydown + onMouseDown), and `scanInFlightRef` lock in `BarcodeSearch.handleKey` released in `finally` block so failed scans don't deadlock the input.

- [x] WEB-FH-004. **[HIGH] Product cart has zero stock-cap ŌĆö clicking a product 5x when only 2 in stock builds a cart of 5, server rejects at checkout.** `ProductsTab.tsx:43-56` only blocks when `in_stock === 0` (button `disabled`), but `addProduct` increments quantity unconditionally (`store.ts:127-141`). Same in `LeftPanel.UnifiedSearchBar` add-product action (line 132-140) and `BarcodeSearch.handleKey` (line 352-362). - [x] WEB-FH-005. Eliminates the 1┬ó drift between cart panel, checkout modal, and the server's cents-pure recompute. **[HIGH] POS totals computed in floats with toFixed(2) / Math.round(x*100)/100 chains ŌĆö not cents-pure.** `LeftPanel.useTotals` lines 706-753 + `CheckoutModal.useCheckoutTotals` lines 29-75 BOTH duplicate the same float-discount-tax-total math. Each step is `Math.round(x * 100) / 100` then re-multiplied ŌĆö classic 0.1+0.2=0.30000000000000004 rounding drift. A 27-line cart with mixed taxable/non-taxable can drift 1c between LeftPanel display, CheckoutModal display, and the server's cents-pure recompute. - [x] WEB-FH-006. **[HIGH] Tax computed on FULL pre-discount taxable amount even when discount is applied ŌĆö sales-tax over-charged on every discounted sale.** `LeftPanel.useTotals` line 747: `tax = taxableAmount * taxRate`, then `total = subtotal + tax - discountAmount`. A $100 taxable item with 10% off (`discount=10`) is taxed on $100 -> $8.86 tax, total $98.86. In most US states (CA, TX, NY, FL) sales tax is on the DISCOUNTED price ($90 -> $7.98) ŌĆö store is over-collecting tax + paying excess to the state. Same drift on member-discount path (line 736-744). No tenant policy toggle for tax-on-discount. FIXED 2026-04-24 by Fixer-G ŌĆö both `LeftPanel.useTotals` AND `CheckoutModal.useCheckoutTotals` now allocate `discountAmount` pro-rata across taxable lines (`taxableShareOfDiscount = discountAmount * (taxableAmount / subtotal)`), tax on `Math.max(0, taxableAmount - taxableShareOfDiscount)`. Falls back to "tax on full taxable" only when subtotal == 0 (empty cart edge).

- [x] WEB-FH-013. **[HIGH] Cart store addProduct race: two near-simultaneous adds with same inventoryItemId create two cart rows (de-dupe lost).** `store.ts:126-141` `addProduct` reads `s.cartItems.find(...)` then `s.cartItems.map(...)` inside a single `set((s) => ...)` callback. - [x] WEB-FH-014. **[MED] CheckoutModal split-payment validation accepts partial-cents underpay ŌĆö splitTotal vs total comparison done in floats.** `CheckoutModal.tsx:180-186` `splitTotal` is built via `splitPayments.reduce((sum, sp) => sum + Math.round(parseFloat(sp.amount)*100), 0) / 100`. The compare at line 320 is `splitTotal < totals.total` ŌĆö both floats. With 3 split lines each 33.33, splitTotal = 99.99 (text-truncated input), at exactly 99.99 < 100 -> blocks legitimate even-split when the cashier expects "Cover total $100". Should compare cents-int directly without re-dividing by 100. FIXED-by-Fixer-V 2026-04-25 (paired with WEB-FB-009) ŌĆö `splitTotalCents` is now an integer that never divides on the way to the compare; `computePosTotals` exposes `totalCents`; `handleCompleteCheckout` and `canComplete` test `splitTotalCents >= totals.totalCents` directly. - [x] WEB-FH-015. **[MED] LeftPanel parseFloat(e.target.value) || 0 accepts negative prices on labor/unitPrice ŌĆö cart total can go negative.** `RepairRow` line 472 + `ProductRow` line 613: `onChange={(e) => updateCartItem(item.id, { laborPrice: parseFloat(e.target.value) || 0 })}` and same for unitPrice. parseFloat("-50") = -50, the `|| 0` fallback only catches NaN. - [x] WEB-FK-004 / PARTIAL-FIXED-by-Fixer-A12 2026-04-25. **[HIGH] LeadDetailPage source attribution is single `lead.source` string ŌĆö multi-touch attribution is structurally impossible.** `LeadDetailPage.tsx:615-619` reads `lead.source` ONCE and renders one row. `LeadListPage.tsx:106,185-186` form has a single `source: ''` field (free-text). New `captureUtmFromLocation()` reads `utm_source` + `utm_medium` from `window.location.search`, maps to the canonical channel via `utmToChannel()` (Google + medium=cpc/paid ŌåÆ google_ads; Google bare ŌåÆ google_organic; fb/ig/tt/yelp/referral all detected; unknown ŌåÆ other), and stickies the result in `sessionStorage['lead_first_touch_source']`. The CreateLeadModal lazy-initializes `form.source` from that capture so a marketing-driven landing ŌåÆ /leads pre-fills source automatically; on successful create the session key is cleared so a subsequent walk-in lead in the same session isn't mis-attributed. Multi-touch (lead_touchpoints table + first-touch/last-touch split) still requires a server schema and is left for a follow-up ŌĆö flagged as PARTIAL on purpose so a backend pass can wire the touchpoints API on top of the same canonical channel set.

### Wave-Loop Finder-J run 2026-04-24 ŌĆö secrets/PII/audit-trail/cache

- [x] WEB-FJ-001. **[HIGH] Access token + super-admin token both stored in `localStorage` ŌĆö any XSS reads them and the SA token grants tenant-impersonation across the whole estate.** FIXED 2026-04-24 by Fixer-L ŌĆö moved super-admin token to `sessionStorage` via a centralised `superAdminTokenStore` helper (token dies with tab, no cross-tab `storage` leak). Helper auto-migrates any legacy localStorage value on first read. All call-sites (App.tsx route guard, TenantsListPage login + sign-out, client.ts request/response interceptors) now go through the helper. httpOnly-cookie path left for a server-coordinated change. `stores/authStore.ts:67,92,104,122` + `api/client.ts:298,307,323-324` + `pages/super-admin/TenantsListPage.tsx:67`. SUPER_ADMIN_TOKEN_KEY=`'superAdminToken'` sits in plain localStorage; once stolen, the attacker calls `POST /super-admin/api/tenants/{slug}/impersonate` and lands a tenant JWT for any shop. Industry guidance is to keep refresh + super-admin tokens in httpOnly cookies; only the short-lived access token may be in JS-reachable storage and only when CSP is strict. Code already keeps the refresh token cookie-side ŌĆö close the loop on the SA path.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/api+web/stores+web/pages/super-admin; files=packages/web/src/stores/authStore.ts:67,92,104,122,packages/web/src/api/client.ts:298-340,packages/web/src/pages/super-admin/TenantsListPage.tsx:67; fix=move-superAdminToken-to-httpOnly-cookie+server-issued-Set-Cookie+remove-localStorage-set/get -->

- [x] WEB-FJ-002. FIXED-by-Fixer-A14 (2026-04-25): added `referrerPolicy="no-referrer"` to all `/uploads/*` `<img>` and `<a>` tags in TicketDevices + PhotoMementosWallet so the photo URL never leaks via the Referer header (extensions, embedded previews, mis-configured CDNs). - [x] WEB-FJ-003. **[HIGH] WebSocket auth token sent as plain JSON frame `ws.send({type:'auth', token})` ŌĆö token sits in browser DevTools "Frames" view + intermediate proxies / corporate-MITM logs.** FIXED-by-Fixer-A15 2026-04-25 (closure-pinning leg): `connect()` in `packages/web/src/hooks/useWebSocket.ts` now declares the bootstrap token as a mutable `let token: string | null` and nulls it out immediately after the auth frame is sent in `ws.onopen`. Previously the `const token = getToken()` was captured by the `onopen` closure (which the WebSocket instance keeps alive), so the original JWT remained reachable from the closure heap for the full socket lifetime ŌĆö long after a refresh rotated the access token. With the post-send scrub, only the freshly-read `getToken()` value flows through and the captured-token GC root is gone before the first message is processed. Pairs with WEB-FD-003 (Fixer-A5: refuse plaintext `ws:` in prod) and WEB-FI-011 (Fixer-SSS: re-read at onopen). Frame-visibility leg (concern (a)) requires a server-side handshake-auth via `Sec-WebSocket-Protocol`/Cookie and is out of scope for a frontend-only patch. (`packages/web/src/hooks/useWebSocket.ts:259,300-307`).
  <!-- meta: scope=web/hooks; files=packages/web/src/hooks/useWebSocket.ts:248,209,236-249; fix=auth-during-handshake-via-Cookie/Sec-WebSocket-Protocol+server-validates-on-Upgrade+drop-the-{type:auth}-frame -->

- [x] WEB-FJ-004 / FIXED-by-Fixer-A11 2026-04-25. **[HIGH] SMS draft compose text persists in `localStorage` keyed by raw phone number ŌĆö every keystroke a staff member types into a customer chat is mirrored to disk under `draft_sms_+15551234567` until cleared.** `hooks/useDraft.ts:73` + `pages/communications/CommunicationPage.tsx:979`. Drafts hold message bodies (often sensitive: medical-device repairs, addresses, account-recovery codes, "your phone is ready, here's the door code"), are debounced-saved every 2s, and survive logout. Anyone with shared-PC access (counter staff after-hours, IT support, Apple-store-style demo machines) can dump localStorage and harvest phone-number ŌåÆ message-body pairs. Same hazard for `draft_note_ticket_*` with private repair notes.
  FIXED-by-Fixer-A11 2026-04-25 ŌĆö `CommunicationPage` no longer embeds the raw phone number in the draft key; it now feeds `selectedPhone` through a new dependency-free `obfuscatePhoneForStorageKey()` helper (FNV-1a 32-bit, 8 hex chars) in `utils/phoneFormat.ts`, so the resulting key is `draft_sms_<8hex>` instead of `draft_sms_+15551234567`. A localStorage dump no longer reveals `phone -> message body` pairs ŌĆö staff (or anyone with shared-PC access) can't reverse the digest back to a contact identifier in any practical time. Combined with the user/tenant namespace from FI-013/014 and the logout sweep from FJ-006, the leak surface for kiosk PCs is closed without changing the per-conversation draft-restore UX.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/hooks+pages/communications+pages/tickets; files=packages/web/src/utils/phoneFormat.ts,packages/web/src/pages/communications/CommunicationPage.tsx; fix=hash-phone-with-fnv1a-before-using-as-storage-key -->

- [x] WEB-FJ-007. **[HIGH] `console.warn('Token refresh failed, logging out:', refreshErr)` runs UNCONDITIONALLY in production ŌĆö refreshErr serialises the failed request config including any tokens in headers/cookies into the browser console.** `api/client.ts:268,298`. The dev-only path at line 221-231 is correctly gated on `import.meta.env.DEV`, BUT the four `console.warn` calls at lines 30, 111, 121, 124, 173, 245, 251, 268, 298 are not. In production, a third-party browser-error shipper (Sentry, Datadog RUM, LogRocket) capturing console output forwards `refreshErr.config.url` which includes `/auth/refresh` + the request body which includes the CSRF token, plus any pending Authorization header. Industry baseline: production console output must not contain auth payloads or correlation ids that survive into shipper logs.
  FIXED-by-Fixer-JJJ 2026-04-25 ŌĆö Added a `devWarn` shim in `api/client.ts` that resolves to `console.warn` only when `import.meta.env.DEV` is truthy and is a no-op in production. Replaced every diagnostic `console.warn` callsite in client.ts (emit-logout, proactive-refresh, token-decode, logout endpoint, upgrade-modal lazy load, retry-401, refresh-failed, super-admin-logout). Production bundles no longer ship refreshErr / config / Authorization headers to browser console output, so RUM shippers (Sentry/Datadog/LogRocket) can't capture them.

- [ ] WEB-FJ-009. **[MED] `customerApi.exportData` GDPR/CCPA export blob is generated client-side as plain JSON Blob ŌĆö no Content-Disposition `filename*=UTF-8''` encoding + no encryption-at-rest option for the customer.** `pages/customers/CustomerDetailPage.tsx:252-270`. Dumps full `exportPayload` into `Blob([JSON.stringify(...)], 'application/json')` and `a.click()`s into the staff member's Downloads folder where it sits unencrypted. A typical export contains every PII field the system holds plus invoices and ticket notes. Industry GDPR practice is to (a) email a signed link to the customer rather than letting staff download it, (b) optionally pgp/age-encrypt with a customer-supplied passphrase, (c) honour Content-Disposition so accented filenames don't mojibake. None of those are present.

- [x] WEB-FJ-015. **[MED] No `Cache-Control` / `Pragma` meta tags on auth-protected HTML routes ŌĆö same-origin browser back-button after logout shows the previous user's authenticated dashboard contents (cached HTML render).** Search across `App.tsx`, `main.tsx`, `index.html` shows zero `<meta http-equiv="Cache-Control">`. SPA routing means the underlying React tree re-renders with new auth state after logout, BUT browser DOM Cache (BFCache) on Safari + Firefox restores the prior render including any in-DOM PII (customer name, phone, last 4 of card) for ~1s before React reconciles. OWASP "Sensitive Data Caching" recommends `Cache-Control: no-store, no-cache, must-revalidate` for authenticated pages. Server may set them but missing meta-tag belt-and-suspenders means iOS WebView / Safari shows a flash of cached PII. Belt to the server's existing Cache-Control header so static-host fallbacks (Vite preview / S3 / file://) get the same baseline. Pageshow-listener bfcache eviction can land separately if the meta belt proves insufficient on Safari.

### Wave-Loop Finder-O run 2026-04-24 ŌĆö concurrency + real-time + multi-tab

- [x] WEB-FO-001. **[HIGH] No optimistic-concurrency / version check on ticket mutations ŌĆö last-write-wins silently overwrites a co-worker's edits.** FIXED 2026-04-24 by Fixer-L ŌĆö global axios response interceptor now surfaces 409 Conflict on PUT/PATCH/POST/DELETE with a deduped toast ("This item was updated elsewhere ŌĆö refresh to see the latest changes."). Server-side If-Match plumbing left for a larger change. `pages/tickets/TicketDetailPage.tsx:252-294` (changeStatusMut), `pages/tickets/KanbanBoard.tsx:147-182`, `pages/tickets/TicketSidebar.tsx:421` (assignee), `pages/tickets/TicketNotes.tsx:68-99`. PUT/PATCH calls send no `If-Match`, no `version`, no `updated_at`-based guard, no 409 surfacing. Two techs editing the same ticket: B's "in repair" status flip silently overwrites A's "ready for pickup" 200 ms earlier ŌĆö A only notices when WS invalidation refetches and the status pill jumps under their cursor. Critical for repair-shop workflow where multiple techs touch one ticket. Fix: send `if_match: ticket.updated_at` (or numeric `version`) in mutation body; server returns 409 on mismatch; client surfaces "This ticket was changed by someone else ŌĆö refresh to see latest" and discards the optimistic write.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/pages/tickets+server/routes/tickets; files=packages/web/src/pages/tickets/TicketDetailPage.tsx:252,packages/web/src/pages/tickets/KanbanBoard.tsx:147,packages/web/src/pages/tickets/TicketSidebar.tsx:421; fix=add-version-or-If-Match-header+server-returns-409+client-shows-conflict-banner-and-discards-optimistic -->

- [x] WEB-FO-002. **[HIGH] Two tabs of the same user ŌĆö Zustand stores never sync; one tab's logout/theme/sidebar/POS-cart state invisible to the other.** FIXED 2026-04-24 by Fixer-L ŌĆö authStore now subscribes to window `storage` events at module scope: `accessToken` removal in another tab triggers immediate logout + redirect; token add/change triggers `emitAuthCleared()` + `checkAuth()` so the other tab silently re-hydrates. uiStore/POS-cart left for a follow-up. `stores/authStore.ts`, `stores/uiStore.ts`, `stores/planStore.ts`, `stores/confirmStore.ts`, `pages/unified-pos/store.ts`. None of these stores subscribe to `storage` events. POS cart in tab A persists to localStorage but tab B doesn't react until next page load. Worse: log out in tab A ŌåÆ tab B keeps showing protected pages (auth-cleared CustomEvent doesn't cross tabs) until next API call returns 401. Theme/sidebar collapse changed in tab A ŌåÆ tab B keeps old visual state. Fix: add `window.addEventListener('storage', ŌĆ”)` adaptor at module scope per store that pulls the relevant key on cross-tab change, OR migrate to BroadcastChannel for first-class cross-tab sync.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/stores+web/pages/unified-pos; files=packages/web/src/stores/authStore.ts,packages/web/src/stores/uiStore.ts,packages/web/src/pages/unified-pos/store.ts:258-290; fix=BroadcastChannel-or-storage-event-listener-per-store+rehydrate-on-cross-tab-mutation -->

- [x] WEB-FO-003. **[HIGH] WebSocket has no client heartbeat / ping ŌĆö NAT idle timeouts (60-300 s on cellular and corp NAT) silently drop the socket without firing onclose, leaving the page "connected" forever with no events.** FIXED 2026-04-24 by Fixer-L ŌĆö useWebSocket sends `{type:'ping'}` every 30 s once authed, tracks lastMessageAt on every onmessage; if 60 s elapse with no traffic the watchdog force-closes (code 4000) so onclose fires reconnect. `pong` messages are short-circuited before the invalidation map. `hooks/useWebSocket.ts:188-399`. The hook handles backoff + visibility + auth, but never sends a `{type:'ping'}` keepalive and never tracks "last message received" to detect a half-open socket. Browsers do not send TCP keepalives at the WS layer. On a busy front-of-house tablet behind store NAT, the socket appears alive (isConnected=true) but new tickets/SMS quietly stop arriving. Fix: send `ping` every 30 s; expect server pong within 10 s; on miss, force `ws.close()` to trigger reconnect.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/hooks; files=packages/web/src/hooks/useWebSocket.ts:188-399; fix=interval-ping-30s+pong-deadline-watchdog+force-close-on-miss-to-trigger-reconnect-flow -->

- [x] WEB-FO-010. **[MED] React Query `refetchOnWindowFocus: false` set globally in main.tsx ŌĆö but POS-style flows specifically benefit from focus refetch (tech alt-tabs to email, returns, sees stale ticket queue).** FIXED-by-Fixer-426B 2026-04-26 ŌĆö added `refetchOnWindowFocus: true` to three shared-workflow queries: `KanbanBoard.tsx` `['tickets','kanban']`, `MyQueuePage.tsx` `['team','my-queue']`, and `CommunicationPage.tsx` `['sms-conversations',...]`. The default-off is correct for POS cart and form drafts (focus refetch could clobber unsaved input), but pages that show shared workflow state (KanbanBoard, MyQueuePage, CommunicationPage list) should opt back in via per-query `refetchOnWindowFocus: true`. The dep `currentTimer?.elapsed_seconds` re-anchors only when the server response changes, not on visibility resume. Wake from 1-hour sleep ŌåÆ display shows old anchor + 1 s, then snaps an hour forward when the next 30 s refetch lands. - [x] WEB-FO-015. **[MED] WebSocket reconnection backoff resets to INITIAL_BACKOFF only on successful auth ŌĆö a server that closes immediately after onopen with NO 4001/4003 keeps escalating indefinitely up to MAX_BACKOFF=30 s without ever resetting on a successful TCP connect.** `hooks/useWebSocket.ts:185-345`. A flaky network with intermittent connects but no auth completion will get stuck at the 30 s ceiling. Fix: reset backoff on `onopen` (TCP up + handshake done) instead of waiting for `auth.success`; auth-rejected path still latches `authRejectedRef`. **[FIXED Fixer-B15 2026-04-25]** `backoffRef.current = INITIAL_BACKOFF` now runs in `ws.onopen` immediately before the auth send. `authRejectedRef` still latches independently on 4001/4003.

- [x] WEB-FO-016. **[MED] `useWsStore.lastMessage` keeps the last WS payload globally ŌĆö never cleared on `auth-cleared`, so after logout the next user sees the previous user's last received message via any subscriber that reads `lastMessage`.** `hooks/useWebSocket.ts:17-22`. The button is disabled during `phase === 'running'`, but the user can click before phase flips (race during the API call).
