The only cross-tab signal is `storage` events (used in `ImpersonationBanner.tsx:65` and `TrainingModeBanner.tsx:37`). Industry standard for this is BroadcastChannel API ("bizarre-crm" channel for auth, "bizarre-pos" channel for cart). Fix: introduce a small `crossTab.ts` helper wrapping BroadcastChannel with a localStorage fallback for Safari < 15.4; route auth-cleared / theme-changed / plan-upgraded through it. ŌĆö Fixer-C15 2026-04-25: added `packages/web/src/utils/crossTab.ts` with a typed `openCrossTabChannel<T>(name)` helper. BroadcastChannel primary path; transient `localStorage` write+remove fallback for Safari < 15.4 / older webviews. Listener errors swallowed per-listener so one bad subscriber can't break siblings. Doc lists the channel-name conventions (`bizarre-crm:auth`, `bizarre-crm:theme`, `bizarre-crm:plan`, `bizarre-pos:cart`, `bizarre-crm:kiosk`). Wiring into `authStore` / `uiStore` / `planStore` is the consumer-side follow-up.

- [x] WEB-FO-019. **[LOW] Header.tsx 30 s setInterval keeps firing while tab is hidden ŌĆö the inner callback gates on `document.visibilityState === 'visible'` so it doesn't actually fetch, but the timer itself still wakes the JS thread every 30 s on tablets left in a back office.** `components/layout/Header.tsx:108`. - [ ] WEB-FO-020. **[LOW] No IndexedDB usage anywhere ŌĆö all client-side cache is in-memory React Query (lost on reload) or 5 MB localStorage. POS receipts, ticket photos, big inventory lists never use IndexedDB even where it would obviously help.** Searched whole repo. Combined with the missing service worker, an "open invoice on a flaky connection" reload always re-fetches everything. - [x] WEB-FO-021. **[LOW] `useDraft` debounces at 2 s but multiple useDraft instances on one form (e.g. Settings has many) each schedule independent timers ŌĆö closing the tab between two timer fires loses work even within debounce window.** `hooks/useDraft.ts:114-149`. Each useDraft mounts its own setTimeout; no `beforeunload` flush. The user types into draft A then draft B, hits cmd-W within 2 s ŌåÆ both timers cancelled, both drafts lost. Fix: register a `beforeunload` listener at module scope that flushes ANY pending `timerRef` for active useDraft instances (track via a Set of refs). ŌĆö @audit-fixed (Fixer-C9 2026-04-25): added module-level `pendingDrafts: Set<PendingDraft>` and a `beforeunload` listener that synchronously walks the set and persists each pending value (respecting the 100 KB quota cap and removing empties). Each `useDraft` instance registers its `{key, getValue}` on debounce-schedule, dedupes via Set semantics, and unregisters on timer fire / value-cleared / unmount. localStorage.setItem is synchronous so the unload write completes safely.

- [ ] WEB-FM-010. **[MED] Three separate `ErrorBoundary` class implementations across the app ŌĆö divergent recovery UX.** `src/main.tsx:57` has a private `ErrorBoundary` (white card + reload button), `src/components/ErrorBoundary.tsx:6` has another `ErrorBoundary` exported and imported by `App.tsx:9` (different fallback markup), and `src/components/shared/PageErrorBoundary.tsx` adds a third with the chunk-reload sentinel logic. The three trees nest (`<ErrorBoundary><AppShell>...<PageErrorBoundary/></AppShell></ErrorBoundary>`), each catching at a different level, with non-uniform "Retry" CTAs and reset behavior. A user who lands on a route-render crash sees the App-level fallback; a render crash inside `<main>` triggers PageErrorBoundary. Pick one canonical class with composable fallback render-prop; delete the other two.

- [x] WEB-FAE-007. **[MED, PARTIAL Fixer-426A 2026-04-26] `Sidebar.tsx:333` `useQuery({ queryKey: ['my-queue', user?.id] })` IS user-scoped, but neighboring `MyQueuePage` (`team/MyQueuePage.tsx:58`) and `TicketHandoffModal.tsx:61` use `['my-queue']` / `['team', 'my-queue']` without `user?.id` ŌĆö three different shapes for one logical query.** CLOSED-by-Fixer-426B 2026-04-26 ŌĆö `DashboardPage.tsx` TechDashboard widget aligned to `['team', 'my-queue']` (was `['my-queue', userId]`). `TicketHandoffModal.tsx` + `TicketDetailPage.tsx` already invalidate `['team', 'my-queue']`. `MyQueuePage.tsx` uses `['team', 'my-queue']`. - [x] WEB-FAE-008. **[MED] `DashboardPage.tsx:1684` `useQuery({ ..., enabled: role === 'manager' })` fetches manager-only team metrics, but if the user logs out and a new admin (not manager) logs in same tab, React Query keeps the previous manager's data cached under the same key and may briefly show it during the moment between `auth-cleared` and the new render.** FIXED-by-Fixer-426B 2026-04-26 ŌĆö `queryKey` changed from `['tech-workload']` to `['tech-workload', role]` so each role has an isolated cache bucket; a role switch always hits a cold cache for that role rather than reading the prior role's stale data. `enabled` only stops fetching, doesn't clear cache. Cache-clear listener at `main.tsx:110` covers this IF event fires; cross-tab path (FAE-004 race) doesn't. Server returns 403 for non-managers but the cached "stale" data still satisfies `useQuery` until `gcTime` expires (default 5min). Fix by adding `role` to the queryKey: `['team-metrics', role]` so manager/admin/tech each have isolated caches.

- [x] WEB-FAE-009. **[MED] `authStore.ts:168` cross-tab storage listener does not validate same-tenant.** FIXED-by-todofixes426 2026-04-26 ŌĆö storage handler reads `tenantSlug` from both old and new JWT payloads (client-side Base64URL decode, no signature verification ŌĆö guard only). On mismatch: clears auth state, dispatches `bizarre-crm:cross-tenant-token` custom event, calls `requestLoginNav()`. `main.tsx` listener catches the custom event and shows a deduped `toast.error('Account changed in another tab')`. Normal same-tenant token rotation (refresh) proceeds unchanged since `oldSlug === newSlug`.

- [x] WEB-FAE-010. **[LOW] `useDraft.ts:46-51` iterates ALL `localStorage` keys to GC old drafts but matches by name pattern only ŌĆö has no tenant/user filter, so a user who logs out leaves draft text (potentially PII / customer notes / SMS body) in localStorage indefinitely until matching keys are GC'd by age.** AUDIT-Fixer-C10 2026-04-25 ŌĆö TODO is stale. `useDraft.ts:40-60` already ships `wipeAllDrafts()` registered as a module-level `bizarre-crm:auth-cleared` listener that walks `localStorage` and removes every key matching `DRAFT_NAMESPACE_LEGACY_RE` (`^bizarrecrm:draft:`). All draft writes are tenant-scoped via `buildScopedKey()` (`bizarrecrm:draft:<userId>:<key>`), so the next user can no longer read prior drafts via DevTools. Closing.
